        <h1 class="page-header">COVID-19 Southern Updates</h1>
<section id="block-contentfield-11" class="node__subtitle block block-fieldblock block-fieldblocknode clearfix">
  
    

      
                        <div class="field field--name-field-subtitle field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field--item"><p><strong>The Southern health system is under Orange under the COVID Protection Framework </strong></p></div>
            
  </section>


  </section>


  </div>

                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
              
            
    </div>

    <section id="block-socialsharelinks" class="promotion promotion--social-share block block-social-share block-social-share-links clearfix">
  
      <h2 class="block-title">Share this</h2>
    

      


<a href="https://www.facebook.com/dialog/share?app_id=455281715120529&amp;name=Share%20on%20facebook&amp;href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.southernhealth.nz%2FCOVID19&amp;caption=&amp;description=&amp;picture=&amp;source=&amp;ref=&amp;display=popup"  target="_blank" data-popup-height="450" class="js-social-share-popup social-share-facebook">
  Share on facebook
</a>



  

<a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet/?text=COVID-19%20Southern%20Updates&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.southernhealth.nz%2FCOVID19&amp;hashtags=&amp;via=southernDHB&amp;related=&amp;in-reply-to="  target="_blank" data-popup-height="300" data-popup-width="500" class="js-social-share-popup social-share-twitter">
  Share with Twitter

  </div>

                          
                                        <div class="region region-content">
    
<section id="block-contentfield-8" class="node__lead prose has-margin-top-base block block-fieldblock block-fieldblocknode clearfix">
  
    

      
                        <div class="field field--name-field-lead field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field--item"><p><strong>The Southern region is at Orange <a href="https://covid19.govt.nz/traffic-lights/life-at-orange/">(COVID Protection Framework)</a>  </strong></p>

<p>Please follow the COVID Protection Framework advice. </p></div>
            
  </section>

  <div class="node node--type-page node--view-mode-full ds-1col clearfix">

  

  <div class="has-margin-top-base prose field field-name-body"><p>To everyone who lives in our district or are planning to come here please get vaccinated, get tested if are sick, and plan ahead. Protect yourself and wear a mask, and please protect our community and health care system.</p>

<p>If people get sick with COVID-19, most will be cared for at home with support from Primary Care teams. If you need to go to hospital we plan to care for most COVID-19 patients at Dunedin Hospital where there is ICU support available. However, all hospitals are planning to care for patients who have COVID -19.</p>

<p><a class="btn btn-lg btn-brand-blue" href="https://www.health.govt.nz/our-work/diseases-and-conditions/covid-19-novel-coronavirus/covid-19-resources-and-tools/nz-covid-tracer-app">NZ COVID tracer app</a> <a class="btn btn-lg btn-brand-blue" href="https://covid19.govt.nz/">Unite Against COVID website</a> <a class="btn btn-lg btn-brand-blue" href="https://www.health.govt.nz/">Ministry of Health website</a></p>
</div>


</div>



  </div>

<section id="block-sdhbemergencycontacts" class="promotion promotion--emergency-contacts block block-block-content block-block-content74b6d36d-d3e5-4030-804c-7a62f2a5669d clearfix">
  
      <h2 class="block-title">Emergency contacts</h2>
    

      
                        <div class="field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field--item"><p>After hours and emergency</br>
<strong><a href="tel:111">111</a></strong></p>

<p>Call Healthline</br>
<strong><a href="tel:0800611116">0800 611 116</a></strong></p>

<p>Call or text Talkline</br>
<strong><a href="tel:1737">1737</a></strong></p>

<p>In a mental health emergency call</br>
<strong><a href="tel:0800 46 78 46">0800 46 78 46</a></strong></p>

<p>Call the National Poisons Centre</br>
<strong><a href="tel:0800 764 766">0800 764 766</a></strong></p>

<p> Call Safe to Talk helpline or text 4334</br>
In the case of sexual harm</br>
<strong><a href="tel:0800 044 334">0800 044 334</a></strong></p>

<p>Call the Family Violence Information Line</br>
<strong><a href="tel:0800 456 450">0800 456 450</a></strong></p>
</div>
            
  </section>
